13 /*

15  * http://csrc.nist.gov/groups/STM/cavp/component-testing.html#ECCCDH
16  * $ sha256sum KAS_ECC_CDH_PrimitiveTest.txt
17  * 456068d3f8aad8ac62a03d19ed3173f00ad51f42b51aeab4753c20f30c01cf23 KAS_ECC_CDH_PrimitiveTest.txt
18  */
19

28 } ecdh_cavs_kat_t;
